UpstreamFilterManager;\n40: class UpstreamCodecFilter;\n41: \n42: /* The Upstream request is the base class for forwarding HTTP upstream.\n43:  *\n44:  * On the new request path, payload (headers/body/metadata/data) still arrives via\n45:  * the accept[X]fromRouter functions. Said data is immediately passed off to the\n46:  * UpstreamFilterManager, which passes each item through the filter chain until\n47:  * it arrives at the last filter in the chain, the UpstreamCodecFilter. If the upstream\n48:  * stream is not established, the UpstreamCodecFilter returns StopAllIteration, and the\n49:  * FilterManager will buffer data, using watermarks to push back to the router\n50:  * filter if buffers become overrun. When an upstream connection is established,\n51:  * the UpstreamCodecFilter will send data upstream.\n52:  *\n53:  * On the new response path, payload arrives from upstream via the UpstreamCodecFilter's\n54:  * CodecBridge. It is passed off directly to the FilterManager, traverses the\n55:  * filter chain, and completion is signaled via the\n56:  * UpstreamRequestFilterManagerCallbacks's encode[X] functions. These somewhat\n57:  * confusingly pass through the UpstreamRequest's legacy decode[X] functions\n58:  * (required due to the UpstreamToDownstream interface, but will be renamed once\n59:  * the classic mode is deprecated), and are finally passed to the router via the\n60:  * RouterFilterInterface onUpstream[X] functions.\n61:  *\n62:  * There is some required communication between the UpstreamRequest and\n63:  * UpstreamCodecFilter. The connection manager bases further\\n36:  * filter invocations on the return code of the previous filter.\\n37:  */\\n38: enum class FilterHeadersStatus {\\n39:   // Continue filter chain iteration.\\n40:   Continue,\\n41:   // Do not iterate for headers on any of the remaining filters in the chain.\\n42:   //\\n43:   // Returning FilterDataStatus::Continue from decodeData()/encodeData() or calling\\n44:   // continueDecoding()/continueEncoding() MUST be called if continued filter iteration is desired.\\n45:   //\\n46:   // Note that if a local reply was sent, no further iteration for headers as well as data and\\n47:   // trailers for the current filter and the filters following will happen. A local reply can be\\n48:   // triggered via sendLocalReply() or encodeHeaders().\\n49:   StopIteration,\\n50:   // Continue headers iteration to remaining filters, but delay ending the stream. This status MUST\\n51:   // NOT be returned when end_stream is already set to false.\\n52:   //\\n53:   // Used when a filter wants to add a body to a headers-only request/response, but this body is not\\n54:   // readily available. Delaying end_stream allows the filter to add the body once it's available\\n55:   // without stopping headers iteration.\\n56:   //\\n57:   // The filter is responsible to continue the stream by providing a body through calling\\n58:   // injectDecodedDataToFilterChain()/injectEncodedDataToFilterChain(), possibly multiple times\\n59:   // if the body needs to be divided into several chunks. The filter may need to handle\\n60:   // watermark events when injecting a body, see:\\n61:   // https://github.com/envoyproxy/envoy/blob/main/source/docs/flow_control.md.\\n62:   //\\n63:   // The last call to inject data MUST have end_stream set to true to conclude the stream.\\n64:   // If the filter cannot provide a body the stream should be reset.\\n65:   //\\n66:   // Adding a body through calling addDecodedData()/addEncodedData() then\\n67:   // continueDecoding()/continueEncoding() is currently NOT supported and causes an assert failure.\\n68:   //\\n69:   // Adding trailers in this scenario is currently NOT supported.\\n70:   //\\n71:   // The filter MUST NOT attempt to continue the stream without providing a body using\\n72:   // continueDecoding()/continueEncoding().\\n73:   //\\n74:   // TODO(yosrym93): Support adding a body in this case by calling addDecodedData()/addEncodedData()\\n75:   // then continueDecoding()/continueEncoding(). To support this a new FilterManager::IterationState\\n76:   // needs to be added and set when a filter returns this status in\\n77:   // FilterManager::decodeHeaders/FilterManager::encodeHeaders()\\n78:   // Currently, when a filter returns this, the IterationState is Continue. {"type":"assistant","message":{"model":"claude-haiku-4-5-20251001","id":"msg_01XbPKzpNZLHGHDJMYsStuXx","type":"message","role":"assistant","content":[{"type":"tool_use","id":"toolu_01H35oyw3DSqr8ifEhxZkUEh","name":"Write","input":{"file_path":"/workspace/documentation.md","content":"# Envoy HTTP Connection Manager Architecture\n\n## Overview\n\nThe HTTP Connection Manager (HCM) is Envoy's central subsystem for processing HTTP requests from downstream clients through to upstream services. This document describes the design and data flow of the four major components that work together to implement request routing and forwarding.\n\n**Repository:** `github.com/envoyproxy/envoy`\n\n---\n\n## 1. ConnectionManagerImpl: The Network Filter\n\n### Component Responsibility\n\n`ConnectionManagerImpl` (source/common/http/conn_manager_impl.h/cc) is a `Network::ReadFilter` that owns the lifecycle of a single downstream connection. It:\n\n- Receives raw TCP/UDP bytes from the network layer via `onData()`\n- Instantiates and manages the appropriate codec (HTTP/1.1, HTTP/2, or HTTP/3)\n- Creates new `ActiveStream` objects for each HTTP request\n- Manages connection-level concerns: drain decisions, overload management, flow control\n- Implements `ServerConnectionCallbacks` to receive streams from the codec\n\n### Key Data Structures\n\n**ActiveStream** (nested struct in conn_manager_impl.h, lines 141-438):\n- Represents a single HTTP request/response pair on a connection\n- Implements `RequestDecoder` to receive decoded request data from the codec\n- Holds the `FilterManager` which executes the per-stream filter chain\n- Tracks stream state including headers, trailers, response encoder\n- Manages local replies and stream-level timeouts\n\n**ConnectionManagerStats**:\n- Metrics for connection counts, request counts, codec events\n- Generated via `generateStats()` static method\n\n### Codec Creation\n\nCodecs are created lazily:\n- For **HTTP/1.1 and HTTP/2**: created on first `onData()` call (lines 84-86)\n- For **HTTP/3**: created on `onConnection()` or when explicitly created via `createCodec()`\n\nThe codec type is determined by protocol negotiation (ALPN for TLS) or static config.\n\n### Connection-Level Flow Control\n\n```\nNetwork receives bytes\n    ↓\nonData(Buffer::Instance& data, bool end_stream)\n    ↓\nCodec parses bytes and generates HTTP frames\n    ↓\nnewStream() creates ResponseEncoder + RequestDecoder pair\n    ↓\nActiveStream.decodeHeaders() → decodeData() → decodeTrailers()\n```\n\n**Watermark Integration** (lines 111-116):\n- `onAboveWriteBufferHighWatermark()`: Propagates to codec, which signals all active streams\n- `onBelowWriteBufferLowWatermark()`: Propagates to codec to resume flow\n- Per-stream watermarks managed by `FilterManager`\n\n### Drain and Overload Management\n\n- **Drain Decision** (Network::DrainDecision): Consulted to gracefully close connections\n- **Overload Manager** (Server::OverloadManager): Monitored for resource exhaustion\n- **Premature Reset Detection**: Tracks rapid stream resets and may drain connection (lines 125-129)\n\n### Source Files\n- **Header**: `source/common/http/conn_manager_impl.h`\n- **Implementation**: `source/common/http/conn_manager_impl.cc`\n- **Config**: `source/common/http/conn_manager_config.h`\n\n---\n\n## 2. FilterManager and the HTTP Filter Chain\n\n### Component Responsibility\n\n`FilterManager` (source/common/http/filter_manager.h/cc) implements per-stream filter chain execution. It:\n\n- Creates the filter chain for each new stream via `FilterChainFactory`\n- Iterates decoder filters on request path (headers → data → trailers)\n- Iterates encoder filters on response path (in reverse order: trailers → data → headers)\n- Manages filter iteration state and buffering\n- Handles filter interactions (filter A can modify headers for filter B)\n- Implements local reply sending when a filter requests it\n\n### Filter Types\n\n**StreamDecoderFilter** (envoy/http/filter.h):\n- Called on request path: `decodeHeaders()`, `decodeData()`, `decodeTrailers()`, `decodeMetadata()`\n- Can stop iteration, modify headers, or send local replies\n- Examples: authentication filter, rate limiting filter\n\n**StreamEncoderFilter** (envoy/http/filter.h):\n- Called on response path: `encode1xxHeaders()`, `encodeHeaders()`, `encodeData()`, `encodeTrailers()`\n- Executed in **reverse** of configuration order (see lines 83-100 in filter_manager.h)\n- Can intercept and modify upstream responses\n- Examples: compression filter, header mutation filter\n\n**StreamFilter** (envoy/http/filter.h, line 1207):\n- Inherits from both `StreamDecoderFilter` and `StreamEncoderFilter`\n- Can process both request and response\n- Examples: router filter, trace filter\n\n### Data Structures\n\n**ActiveStreamFilterBase** (lines 109-235):\n- Wrapper for each filter in the chain\n- Manages iteration state: `Continue`, `StopSingleIteration`, `StopAllBuffer`, `StopAllWatermark`\n- Handles buffering and state transitions\n- Common logic for `decodeHeaders()`, `decodeData()`, etc.\n\n**StreamDecoderFilters** (lines 73-81):\n- Vector of `ActiveStreamDecoderFilter` entries\n- Forward iteration during request processing\n\n**StreamEncoderFilters** (lines 92-100):\n- Vector of `ActiveStreamEncoderFilter` entries\n- Reverse iteration during response processing (ensures filters run in reverse config order)\n\n### Request Path Flow\n\n```\nCodec parses bytes → newStream() called\n    ↓\nActiveStream.decodeHeaders(RequestHeaderMapSharedPtr headers, bool end_stream)\n    ↓\nFilterManager.decodeHeaders() called\n    ↓\nFor each StreamDecoderFilter in sequence:\n    - Filter A.decodeHeaders() → returns FilterHeadersStatus\n    - If StopIteration: stop, buffer subsequent frames\n    - If Continue: proceed to next filter\n    ↓\nLast filter (router) processes headers, initiates upstream request\n    ↓\nIf all filters returned Continue:\n    ActiveStream.decodeData() called for each chunk\n    ↓\n    For each filter: decodeData() → returns FilterDataStatus\n    (Similar iteration logic)\n    ↓\n    ActiveStream.decodeTrailers() called (if present)\n```\n\n### Response Path Flow\n\n```\nUpstream sends response headers\n    ↓\nUpstreamRequest.decodeHeaders() called (translates to response)\n    ↓\nFilterManager.encodeHeaders() called\n    ↓\nFor each StreamEncoderFilter in REVERSE sequence:\n    - Filter C.encodeHeaders()\n    - Filter B.encodeHeaders()\n    - Filter A.encodeHeaders()\n    ↓\nResponse encoder sends headers downstream to codec\n    ↓\nSame reverse iteration for data and trailers\n```\n\n### Filter Iteration State Management\n\n**IterationState enum** (lines 211-218):\n- `Continue`: Normal iteration\n- `StopSingleIteration`: Stop only for current frame type (headers/data/trailers)\n- `StopAllBuffer`: Stop for all frame types, buffer data\n- `StopAllWatermark`: Stop for all frame types, use watermark-based push-back\n\nWhen a filter returns `StopIteration`:\n1. Current filter continues processing that frame type\n2. Subsequent filters skip that frame type\n3. When `continueDecoding()` is called, iteration resumes from current filter\n\n### Key Callbacks\n\n**StreamFilterCallbacks** (accessed by filters):\n- `streamInfo()`: Access request/response metadata\n- `connection()`: Get downstream connection info\n- `resetStream()`: Trigger stream reset\n- `sendLocalReply()`: Send error response directly to client\n- `encodeHeaders()`, `encodeData()`, `encodeTrailers()`: Filters can encode responses\n\n### Source Files\n- **Header**: `source/common/http/filter_manager.h`\n- **Implementation**: `source/common/http/filter_manager.cc`\n- **Factory Config**: `source/common/http/conn_manager_config.h`\n\n---\n\n## 3. Router Filter: Route Selection and Upstream Dispatch\n\n### Component Responsibility\n\nThe Router filter (source/common/router/router.h/cc, configured in source/extensions/filters/http/router/config.cc) is the terminal decoder filter. It:\n\n- Consults `RouteConfiguration` to select the target cluster for each request\n- Obtains an HTTP connection pool from `ClusterManager`\n- Creates and manages `UpstreamRequest` objects for request forwarding\n- Implements retry logic, timeouts, and hedged requests\n- Transforms downstream request into upstream request (protocol conversion, header modification)\n- Manages the request lifecycle until upstream response arrives\n\n### Route Selection\n\n```\nRouter.decodeHeaders(RequestHeaderMap& headers, bool end_stream)\n    ↓\nRoute selection logic:\n    1. Consult scoped route config (from RDS)\n    2. Match request path, method, headers against configured routes\n    3. Select RouteEntry (one of: cluster route, weighted cluster, redirect, etc.)\n    ↓\nRouteEntry determines:\n    - Target cluster name\n    - Timeout policy\n    - Retry policy\n    - Header mutations\n    - Load balancing policy\n    - Metadata matching criteria\n```\n\nThe route configuration is obtained from:\n- **Static routes** in bootstrap config\n- **Dynamic routes** via RDS (Route Discovery Service)\n- **Scoped routes** for per-request route selection (e.g., by header value)\n\n### UpstreamRequest Creation\n\nOnce a cluster is selected:\n\n```\nClusterManager.getThreadLocalCluster(cluster_name)\n    ↓\nThreadLocalCluster provides:\n    - Load balancer instance\n    - HTTP connection pool factory\n    ↓\nLoad balancer selects a host from cluster's healthy endpoints\n    ↓\nHTTP connection pool is obtained for the selected host\n    ↓\nUpstreamRequest created with:\n    - Conn pool (GenericConnPool)\n    - Parent router filter\n    - Stream options (timeouts, retries, etc.)\n```\n\n### UpstreamRequest Lifecycle\n\n**UpstreamRequest** (source/common/router/upstream_request.h/cc):\n\n1. **Connection Pool Phase**:\n   - Request is queued in connection pool if no connection available\n   - Pool creates new connection or reuses idle connection\n   - Once connection ready, `onPoolReady()` is called\n\n2. **Upstream Request Setup**:\n   ```\n   onPoolReady(GenericUpstream upstream, HostDescriptionConstSharedPtr host)\n       ↓\n   Create upstream filter manager (UpstreamFilterManager)\n       ↓\n   acceptHeadersFromRouter() passes request through upstream filters\n       ↓\n   UpstreamCodecFilter sends headers to upstream codec\n       ↓\n   Upstream codec encodes to bytes and sends on connection\n   ```\n\n3. **Upstream Response Phase**:\n   - Upstream codec parses response bytes\n   - Response decoder calls `decodeHeaders()`, `decodeData()`, `decodeTrailers()`\n   - Data passes through upstream filter chain (reverse of downstream)\n   - `UpstreamToDownstream` interface translates to downstream response path\n\n4. **Completion**:\n   - UpstreamRequest tracks per-try timeout and global timeout\n   - On timeout or upstream error: implements retry logic\n   - Retry state decides if request can be retried to different host\n   - After max retries or success, response sent downstream\n\n### Retry Logic\n\n**RetryState** (source/common/router/retry_state_impl.h/cc):\n- Evaluates retry-able errors (connection failure, 5xx status, specific headers)\n- Tracks retry count against configured policy\n- Selects different host on retry to avoid bad endpoints\n- Implements exponential backoff for per-try timeouts\n\n### Timeout Handling\n\n- **Global timeout**: Entire request-response must complete within this time\n- **Per-try timeout**: Each upstream attempt has this timeout\n- **Hedged requests**: If per-try timeout expires, start another request to different host (if configured)\n\n### Shadow Routing\n\nThe router can send \"shadow\" copies of requests to alternate clusters for testing:\n```\nRoute has shadow policy (target cluster + sample rate)\n    ↓\nRouter filter checks if request should be shadowed (random based on sample rate)\n    ↓\nShadowWriter creates secondary upstream request to shadow cluster\n    ↓\nShadow response is discarded (not returned to client)\n    ↓\nOriginal response returned normally\n```\n\n### LoadBalancerContext\n\nThe Filter class implements `Upstream::LoadBalancerContextBase` to provide context for load balancing decisions:\n- Requested cluster info\n- Hash policy and hash key computation\n- Metadata matching criteria\n- Retry state (for host selection during retries)\n- Override host selection\n\n### Source Files\n- **Main Filter**: `source/common/router/router.h` (Filter, FilterConfig classes)\n- **Router Config**: `source/common/router/config_impl.h/cc` (RouteConfiguration parsing)\n- **Route Matching**: `source/common/router/config_impl.h` (RouteEntry, VirtualHost, Cluster match logic)\n- **Upstream Request**: `source/common/router/upstream_request.h/cc`\n- **Retry State**: `source/common/router/retry_state_impl.h/cc`\n- **HTTP Filter Config**: `source/extensions/filters/http/router/config.h/cc`\n\n---\n\n## 4. Cluster Manager and Upstream Connectivity\n\n### Component Responsibility\n\n`ClusterManager` (source/common/upstream/cluster_manager_impl.h/cc) is the subsystem managing upstream clusters and their connection pools. It:\n\n- Maintains cluster definitions and their health state\n- Provides HTTP/TCP connection pools per cluster-host pair\n- Interfaces with load balancers to select healthy hosts\n- Integrates health checking and outlier detection\n- Manages dynamic cluster discovery via CDS (Cluster Discovery Service)\n- Tracks cluster statistics (connection counts, failures, timeouts)\n\n### Cluster Hierarchy\n\n```\nClusterManager\n    ↓\n    Map<cluster_name, ClusterInfo>\n        ↓\n        ClusterInfo:\n            - Cluster configuration (timeout, protocol, TLS settings)\n            - Load balancer instance\n            - Health checker instance\n            - Priority set (primary, secondary, etc.)\n```\n\n### Load Balancing\n\n**Cluster** → **PrioritySet** → **HealthyLoad** → **Host**\n\n1. **Load Balancer Instance** (`Upstream::LoadBalancer`):\n   - Selects host from cluster based on load balancing algorithm\n   - Algorithms: round-robin, least-request, ring-hash, maglev, etc.\n   - Called from router filter with `LoadBalancerContext`\n\n2. **Priority Set**:\n   - Clusters can be organized by priority (primary, backup, etc.)\n   - Load balancer first tries to select from highest-priority healthy hosts\n   - Falls back to lower priorities if higher-priority unavailable\n   - Prevents over-load of primary cluster during failures\n\n3. **Host Selection**:\n   ```\n   LoadBalancer.chooseHost(LoadBalancerContext& context)\n       ↓\n   Compute hash key if using hash policy\n       ↓\n   Apply metadata matching (route metadata + request metadata + connection metadata)\n       ↓\n   Select host from priority set respecting health status\n       ↓\n   Return HostDescriptionConstSharedPtr\n   ```\n\n### Connection Pool Architecture\n\n**HTTP Connection Pool** (`Http::ConnectionPool::Instance`):\n- Per host, per protocol\n- Manages HTTP/1.1, HTTP/2, or HTTP/3 connections to a single upstream host\n- Reuses idle connections\n- Multiplexes multiple streams (for HTTP/2+)\n\n```\nClusterManager::getConnPool(cluster, host, protocol)\n    ↓\nThreadLocalCluster looks up in connection pool map\n    ↓\nIf not found:\n    Create HttpConnPoolImplBase (or HTTP/2 variant)\n    ↓\n    Stores in connection pool map\n    ↓\nHTTP Connection Pool.newStream(ResponseDecoder, Callbacks)\n    ↓\n    If connection available:\n        Attach stream to connection\n        Call Callbacks.onPoolReady()\n    ↓\n    If connection not available but space in queue:\n        Create PendingStream, enqueue\n    ↓\n    If queue full (overload):\n        Call Callbacks.onPoolFailure()\n```\n\n### Connection Lifecycle\n\n**ActiveClient** (managed by HttpConnPoolImplBase):\n```\nCreate connection to host\n    ↓\nCreate codec client (Http1CodecClient or Http2CodecClient)\n    ↓\nEstablish TCP/TLS connection\n    ↓\nFor HTTP/2: send preface and settings\n    ↓\nAccept new streams:\n    For each newStream() request:\n        Get RequestEncoder from codec\n        Attach ResponseDecoder\n        Pass upstream bytes to decoder\n        Return upstream response\n    ↓\nConnection idle timeout → destroy if no active streams\n    ↓\nMax lifetime reached → gracefully drain (complete in-flight, then close)\n```\n\n### Health Checking and Outlier Detection\n\n**Health Checker** (source/common/upstream/health_checker_impl.h/cc):\n- Periodically probes upstream hosts\n- Updates host health status (healthy, degraded, unhealthy)\n- Notifies load balancer when status changes\n\n**Outlier Detection** (source/common/upstream/outlier_detection_impl.h/cc):\n- Monitors request failures to detect failing hosts\n- Ejects unhealthy hosts from load balancer pool\n- Periodically checks if ejected hosts recovered\n- Algorithms: success rate, consecutive failures, HTTP status codes\n\nLoad balancer respects health state:\n```\nLoad Balancer.chooseHost()\n    ↓\n    For each candidate host:\n        If health_status == Healthy: weight = 100%\n        If health_status == Degraded: weight = partial\n        If health_status == Unhealthy: weight = 0% (skip unless no other choice)\n    ↓\n    Select host with probability weighted by health\n```\n\n### Dynamic Cluster Discovery (CDS)\n\nClusters can be added/updated dynamically:\n\n```\nCDS Config Source configured\n    ↓\nClusterManager subscribes to CDS updates\n    ↓\nControl plane sends Cluster proto messages\n    ↓\nClusterManager.addOrUpdateCluster()\n    ↓\n    Parse cluster proto\n    ↓\n    Create new ClusterInfo with appropriate load balancer factory\n    ↓\n    Notify subscribers (e.g., router) of cluster change\n```\n\n### Statistics\n\nConnection pool and upstream statistics tracked:\n- `upstream_cx_total`: Total connections created\n- `upstream_cx_active`: Currently active connections\n- `upstream_rq_total`: Total requests\n- `upstream_rq_pending`: Requests waiting for connection\n- `upstream_rq_time`: Request latency histogram\n- Failures: connect failures, timeouts, reset counts\n- Per-host health status metrics\n\n### Source Files\n- **Main Manager**: `source/common/upstream/cluster_manager_impl.h/cc`\n- **Cluster Info**: `source/common/upstream/upstream_impl.h/cc`\n- **Connection Pools**:\n  - Base: `source/common/http/conn_pool_base.h/cc`\n  - HTTP/1: `source/common/http/http1/conn_pool.h/cc`\n  - HTTP/2: `source/common/http/http2/conn_pool.h/cc`\n- **Load Balancers**: `source/common/upstream/load_*_lb.cc` (various algorithms)\n- **Health Checking**: `source/common/upstream/health_checker_impl.h/cc`\n- **Outlier Detection**: `source/common/upstream/outlier_detection_impl.h/cc`\n\n---\n\n## End-to-End Request Flow\n\n### Complete Request Journey\n\n```\n1. TCP SYN arrives at downstream listener\n   ConnectionManagerImpl.onNewConnection()\n   ↓\n2. Client sends HTTP request bytes\n   ConnectionManagerImpl.onData(data, end_stream)\n   ↓\n3. Codec parses bytes (HTTP/1, HTTP/2, or HTTP/3)\n   Codec.onServerData(Buffer)\n   ↓\n4. Codec emits decoded request\n   ServerConnectionCallbacks.newStream(ResponseEncoder)\n   ↓\n5. ConnectionManagerImpl creates ActiveStream\n   RequestDecoder = ActiveStream\n   ResponseEncoder from codec\n   ↓\n6. Codec calls ActiveStream.decodeHeaders(headers, end_stream)\n   ↓\n7. ActiveStream.decodeHeaders calls FilterManager.decodeHeaders()\n   ↓\n8. FilterManager iterates decoder filters (router is last)\n   Filter A.decodeHeaders() → Filter B.decodeHeaders() → Router.decodeHeaders()\n   ↓\n9. Router filter:\n   - Selects route and cluster\n   - Calls ClusterManager to get connection pool\n   - Creates UpstreamRequest\n   ↓\n10. Connection pool status:\n    If connection available:\n        onPoolReady() called immediately\n    Else:\n        Request queued, waiting for connection\n        On connection ready: onPoolReady() called\n   ↓\n11. UpstreamRequest.onPoolReady():\n    - Creates GenericUpstream (HTTP codec for upstream)\n    - Calls acceptHeadersFromRouter(end_stream)\n    ↓\n12. Data flows through upstream filter chain\n    UpstreamCodecFilter encodes to upstream bytes\n    Bytes sent on upstream connection\n    ↓\n13. Upstream server processes and sends response\n    Response bytes arrive on upstream connection\n    ↓\n14. Upstream codec parses response\n    Calls UpstreamRequest.decodeHeaders() (response)\n    ↓\n15. Router filter translates upstream response to downstream format\n    Calls encodeHeaders() on downstream encoder\n    ↓\n16. FilterManager iterates encoder filters in reverse\n    Filter C.encodeHeaders() → Filter B.encodeHeaders() → Filter A.encodeHeaders()\n    ↓\n17. Last filter's encodeHeaders() calls ResponseEncoder.encodeHeaders()\n    ↓\n18. Downstream codec encodes headers to bytes\n    Sends to client\n    ↓\n19. Upstream response body chunks\n    Each chunk flows through:\n    Router.onUpstreamData(data) → encodeData() → Filter chain → ResponseEncoder\n    ↓\n20. Upstream closes or sends trailers\n    UpstreamRequest.decodeTrailers() called\n    ↓\n21. Router and filter chain process trailers\n    ResponseEncoder.encodeTrailers()\n    ↓\n22. Codec sends trailers to client\n    ↓\n23. Stream complete\n    ActiveStream.completeRequest()\n    Access logs written\n    Metrics updated\n    Stream destroyed\n```\n\n### Request Path Summary\n\n```\nNetwork\n  ↓\nConnectionManagerImpl.onData()\n  ↓\nCodec\n  ↓\nActiveStream.decodeHeaders/Data/Trailers\n  ↓\nFilterManager (decoder filters)\n  ↓\nRouter Filter\n  ↓\nClusterManager + Load Balancer\n  ↓\nHTTP Connection Pool\n  ↓\nUpstream Codec\n  ↓\nUpstream Connection\n```\n\n### Response Path Summary\n\n```\nUpstream Connection\n  ↓\nUpstream Codec\n  ↓\nUpstreamRequest.decodeHeaders/Data/Trailers\n  ↓\nRouter Filter (response translator)\n  ↓\nFilterManager (encoder filters in reverse)\n  ↓\nResponseEncoder\n  ↓\nDownstream Codec\n  ↓\nNetwork (to client)\n```\n\n---\n\n## Extension Points\n\n### 1. Custom Filters\n\nImplement `StreamDecoderFilter`, `StreamEncoderFilter`, or `StreamFilter`:\n\n```cpp\nclass MyCustomFilter : public Http::StreamDecoderFilter {\n  // Process request headers\n  Http::FilterHeadersStatus decodeHeaders(\n      Http::RequestHeaderMap& headers, bool end_stream) override {\n    // Modify headers, check authentication, rate limit, etc.\n    return Http::FilterHeadersStatus::Continue;\n  }\n\n  // Process request body\n  Http::FilterDataStatus decodeData(\n      Buffer::Instance& data, bool end_stream) override {\n    return Http::FilterDataStatus::Continue;\n  }\n};\n```\n\nRegistered via `HttpFilterConfigFactory` and included in HCM config.\n\n### 2. Route Configuration\n\nExtend `RouteConfiguration` to add custom route matching:\n- Custom header matchers\n- Custom metadata matching criteria\n- Custom cluster selection logic\n\n### 3. Cluster Extensions\n\nImplement custom load balancing algorithms via `ThreadAwareLoadBalancer`:\n- Custom selection logic respecting health state\n- Custom host weighting strategies\n\n### 4. Access Loggers\n\nImplement `AccessLog::Instance` to log request/response pairs:\n- Runs after stream completion\n- Access to full request, response, and stream info\n\n### 5. HTTP Codecs\n\nImplement custom codec for new HTTP protocol versions:\n```cpp\nclass MyHttpCodec : public Http::ServerConnection {\n  // Handle new protocol\n};\n```\n\n### 6. Health Checkers\n\nCustom upstream health check logic:\n```cpp\nclass MyHealthChecker : public Upstream::HealthChecker {\n  // Probe upstream hosts\n};\n```\n\n---\n\n## Error Handling\n\n### Codec Errors\nIf codec fails to parse:\n- Exception raised\n- ConnectionManagerImpl catches\n- Local reply: 400 Bad Request or 426 Upgrade Required\n- Connection may be closed\n\n### Filter Errors\nIf filter raises exception during decoding:\n- FilterManager catches\n- Local reply: 500 Internal Server Error\n- Filter is considered in error state\n- Subsequent filters may skip\n\n### Upstream Errors\nIf upstream connection fails:\n- UpstreamRequest.onPoolFailure() called\n- Router evaluates retry policy\n- If retryable: select new host, try again\n- If non-retryable or retries exhausted: send error response (502/503/504)\n\n### Local Reply Flow\nIf a filter (or router) calls `sendLocalReply()`:\n1. Headers and body created\n2. Response encoder calls ResponseEncoder.encodeHeaders()\n3. Downstream codec encodes to bytes\n4. Client receives error response\n5. Stream ends (no further data processing)\n\n---\n\n## Performance Considerations\n\n### Stream Multiplexing\n- HTTP/2+ supports multiple concurrent streams per connection\n- Each stream has independent state, timers, filters\n- Load balancer distributes streams across connection pool\n\n### Connection Pooling\n- Reuse connections to reduce handshake overhead\n- Connection pool limits prevent connection storms\n- Idle timeout prevents resource leaks\n\n### Buffering Strategy\n- Filters can buffer data (e.g., for request body inspection)\n- Watermarks prevent memory exhaustion\n- Small buffers are preferred; large requests chunked\n\n### Timeout Configuration\n- Global timeout: conservative (e.g., 30 seconds)\n- Per-try timeout: shorter (e.g., 5-10 seconds per retry)\n- Allows quick failure detection without excessive latency\n\n---\n\n## Key Interfaces and Their Relationships\n\n```\nNetwork::ReadFilter (ConnectionManagerImpl)\n    ↓ creates\nActive Streams\n    ↓ uses\nFilterManager\n    ↓ chains\nStreamDecoderFilter (router is last)\n    ↓ calls\nRouter Filter\n    ↓ uses\nClusterManager\n    ↓ provides\nLoadBalancer\n    ↓ selects\nHost\n    ↓ provides pool to\nHTTP Connection Pool\n    ↓ creates\nUpstream Codec\n    ↓ sends to/receives from\nUpstream Connection\n```\n\n---\n\n## Related Configuration\n\nKey HCM configuration (envoy/extensions/filters/network/http_connection_manager/v3/http_connection_manager.proto):\n\n- `route_config`: Static route configuration\n- `rds`: Dynamic route discovery config\n- `http_filters`: List of filter configs (order matters for decoder)\n- `access_log`: Access log configuration\n- `common_http_protocol_options`: Timeouts, connection limits\n- `http_protocol_options`: HTTP/1-specific settings\n- `http2_protocol_options`: HTTP/2-specific settings\n- `tracing`: Distributed tracing configuration\n- `stats_matches`: Metrics configuration\n\n---\n\n## Summary\n\nThe HTTP Connection Manager processes requests through a layered architecture:\n\n1. **ConnectionManagerImpl** owns the network connection and creates request streams\n2. **FilterManager** chains request through user-defined filters and the router\n3. **Router Filter** selects the upstream cluster and initiates the upstream request\n4. **ClusterManager** provides connection pooling and load balancing to upstream hosts\n\nEach component has clear responsibilities and well-defined interfaces, enabling Envoy's extensibility through filters, load balancers, health checkers, and codec implementations. The request flows through decoder filters on entry, through the router for cluster selection, through the upstream connection pool, and back through encoder filters on response.\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":12,"cache_creation_input_tokens":4009,"cache_read_input_tokens":74696,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":4009},"output_tokens":1,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"c6eb6864-3919-41b8-a854-df0bcc2da3da","uuid":"652f657c-bd7c-47d9-948d-1b9921b82aaf"}

This document describes the design and data flow of the four major components that work together to implement request routing and forwarding.\n\n**Repository:** `github.com/envoyproxy/envoy`\n\n---\n\n## 1. ConnectionManagerImpl: The Network Filter\n\n### Component Responsibility\n\n`ConnectionManagerImpl` (source/common/http/conn_manager_impl.h/cc) is a `Network::ReadFilter` that owns the lifecycle of a single downstream connection. It:\n\n- Receives raw TCP/UDP bytes from the network layer via `onData()`\n- Instantiates and manages the appropriate codec (HTTP/1.1, HTTP/2, or HTTP/3)\n- Creates new `ActiveStream` objects for each HTTP request\n- Manages connection-level concerns: drain decisions, overload management, flow control\n- Implements `ServerConnectionCallbacks` to receive streams from the codec\n\n### Key Data Structures\n\n**ActiveStream** (nested struct in conn_manager_impl.h, lines 141-438):\n- Represents a single HTTP request/response pair on a connection\n- Implements `RequestDecoder` to receive decoded request data from the codec\n- Holds the `FilterManager` which executes the per-stream filter chain\n- Tracks stream state including headers, trailers, response encoder\n- Manages local replies and stream-level timeouts\n\n**ConnectionManagerStats**:\n- Metrics for connection counts, request counts, codec events\n- Generated via `generateStats()` static method\n\n### Codec Creation\n\nCodecs are created lazily:\n- For **HTTP/1.1 and HTTP/2**: created on first `onData()` call (lines 84-86)\n- For **HTTP/3**: created on `onConnection()` or when explicitly created via `createCodec()`\n\nThe codec type is determined by protocol negotiation (ALPN for TLS) or static config.\n\n### Connection-Level Flow Control\n\n```\nNetwork receives bytes\n    ↓\nonData(Buffer::Instance& data, bool end_stream)\n    ↓\nCodec parses bytes and generates HTTP frames\n    ↓\nnewStream() creates ResponseEncoder + RequestDecoder pair\n    ↓\nActiveStream.decodeHeaders() → decodeData() → decodeTrailers()\n```\n\n**Watermark Integration** (lines 111-116):\n- `onAboveWriteBufferHighWatermark()`: Propagates to codec, which signals all active streams\n- `onBelowWriteBufferLowWatermark()`: Propagates to codec to resume flow\n- Per-stream watermarks managed by `FilterManager`\n\n### Drain and Overload Management\n\n- **Drain Decision** (Network::DrainDecision): Consulted to gracefully close connections\n- **Overload Manager** (Server::OverloadManager): Monitored for resource exhaustion\n- **Premature Reset Detection**: Tracks rapid stream resets and may drain connection (lines 125-129)\n\n### Source Files\n- **Header**: `source/common/http/conn_manager_impl.h`\n- **Implementation**: `source/common/http/conn_manager_impl.cc`\n- **Config**: `source/common/http/conn_manager_config.h`\n\n---\n\n## 2. FilterManager and the HTTP Filter Chain\n\n### Component Responsibility\n\n`FilterManager` (source/common/http/filter_manager.h/cc) implements per-stream filter chain execution. It:\n\n- Creates the filter chain for each new stream via `FilterChainFactory`\n- Iterates decoder filters on request path (headers → data → trailers)\n- Iterates encoder filters on response path (in reverse order: trailers → data → headers)\n- Manages filter iteration state and buffering\n- Handles filter interactions (filter A can modify headers for filter B)\n- Implements local reply sending when a filter requests it\n\n### Filter Types\n\n**StreamDecoderFilter** (envoy/http/filter.h):\n- Called on request path: `decodeHeaders()`, `decodeData()`, `decodeTrailers()`, `decodeMetadata()`\n- Can stop iteration, modify headers, or send local replies\n- Examples: authentication filter, rate limiting filter\n\n**StreamEncoderFilter** (envoy/http/filter.h):\n- Called on response path: `encode1xxHeaders()`, `encodeHeaders()`, `encodeData()`, `encodeTrailers()`\n- Executed in **reverse** of configuration order (see lines 83-100 in filter_manager.h)\n- Can intercept and modify upstream responses\n- Examples: compression filter, header mutation filter\n\n**StreamFilter** (envoy/http/filter.h, line 1207):\n- Inherits from both `StreamDecoderFilter` and `StreamEncoderFilter`\n- Can process both request and response\n- Examples: router filter, trace filter\n\n### Data Structures\n\n**ActiveStreamFilterBase** (lines 109-235):\n- Wrapper for each filter in the chain\n- Manages iteration state: `Continue`, `StopSingleIteration`, `StopAllBuffer`, `StopAllWatermark`\n- Handles buffering and state transitions\n- Common logic for `decodeHeaders()`, `decodeData()`, etc.\n\n**StreamDecoderFilters** (lines 73-81):\n- Vector of `ActiveStreamDecoderFilter` entries\n- Forward iteration during request processing\n\n**StreamEncoderFilters** (lines 92-100):\n- Vector of `ActiveStreamEncoderFilter` entries\n- Reverse iteration during response processing (ensures filters run in reverse config order)\n\n### Request Path Flow\n\n```\nCodec parses bytes → newStream() called\n    ↓\nActiveStream.decodeHeaders(RequestHeaderMapSharedPtr headers, bool end_stream)\n    ↓\nFilterManager.decodeHeaders() called\n    ↓\nFor each StreamDecoderFilter in sequence:\n    - Filter A.decodeHeaders() → returns FilterHeadersStatus\n    - If StopIteration: stop, buffer subsequent frames\n    - If Continue: proceed to next filter\n    ↓\nLast filter (router) processes headers, initiates upstream request\n    ↓\nIf all filters returned Continue:\n    ActiveStream.decodeData() called for each chunk\n    ↓\n    For each filter: decodeData() → returns FilterDataStatus\n    (Similar iteration logic)\n    ↓\n    ActiveStream.decodeTrailers() called (if present)\n```\n\n### Response Path Flow\n\n```\nUpstream sends response headers\n    ↓\nUpstreamRequest.decodeHeaders() called (translates to response)\n    ↓\nFilterManager.encodeHeaders() called\n    ↓\nFor each StreamEncoderFilter in REVERSE sequence:\n    - Filter C.encodeHeaders()\n    - Filter B.encodeHeaders()\n    - Filter A.encodeHeaders()\n    ↓\nResponse encoder sends headers downstream to codec\n    ↓\nSame reverse iteration for data and trailers\n```\n\n### Filter Iteration State Management\n\n**IterationState enum** (lines 211-218):\n- `Continue`: Normal iteration\n- `StopSingleIteration`: Stop only for current frame type (headers/data/trailers)\n- `StopAllBuffer`: Stop for all frame types, buffer data\n- `StopAllWatermark`: Stop for all frame types, use watermark-based push-back\n\nWhen a filter returns `StopIteration`:\n1. Current filter continues processing that frame type\n2. Subsequent filters skip that frame type\n3. When `continueDecoding()` is called, iteration resumes from current filter\n\n### Key Callbacks\n\n**StreamFilterCallbacks** (accessed by filters):\n- `streamInfo()`: Access request/response metadata\n- `connection()`: Get downstream connection info\n- `resetStream()`: Trigger stream reset\n- `sendLocalReply()`: Send error response directly to client\n- `encodeHeaders()`, `encodeData()`, `encodeTrailers()`: Filters can encode responses\n\n### Source Files\n- **Header**: `source/common/http/filter_manager.h`\n- **Implementation**: `source/common/http/filter_manager.cc`\n- **Factory Config**: `source/common/http/conn_manager_config.h`\n\n---\n\n## 3. Router Filter: Route Selection and Upstream Dispatch\n\n### Component Responsibility\n\nThe Router filter (source/common/router/router.h/cc, configured in source/extensions/filters/http/router/config.cc) is the terminal decoder filter. It:\n\n- Consults `RouteConfiguration` to select the target cluster for each request\n- Obtains an HTTP connection pool from `ClusterManager`\n- Creates and manages `UpstreamRequest` objects for request forwarding\n- Implements retry logic, timeouts, and hedged requests\n- Transforms downstream request into upstream request (protocol conversion, header modification)\n- Manages the request lifecycle until upstream response arrives\n\n### Route Selection\n\n```\nRouter.decodeHeaders(RequestHeaderMap& headers, bool end_stream)\n    ↓\nRoute selection logic:\n    1. Consult scoped route config (from RDS)\n    2. Match request path, method, headers against configured routes\n    3. Select RouteEntry (one of: cluster route, weighted cluster, redirect, etc.)\n    ↓\nRouteEntry determines:\n    - Target cluster name\n    - Timeout policy\n    - Retry policy\n    - Header mutations\n    - Load balancing policy\n    - Metadata matching criteria\n```\n\nThe route configuration is obtained from:\n- **Static routes** in bootstrap config\n- **Dynamic routes** via RDS (Route Discovery Service)\n- **Scoped routes** for per-request route selection (e.g., by header value)\n\n### UpstreamRequest Creation\n\nOnce a cluster is selected:\n\n```\nClusterManager.getThreadLocalCluster(cluster_name)\n    ↓\nThreadLocalCluster provides:\n    - Load balancer instance\n    - HTTP connection pool factory\n    ↓\nLoad balancer selects a host from cluster's healthy endpoints\n    ↓\nHTTP connection pool is obtained for the selected host\n    ↓\nUpstreamRequest created with:\n    - Conn pool (GenericConnPool)\n    - Parent router filter\n    - Stream options (timeouts, retries, etc.)\n```\n\n### UpstreamRequest Lifecycle\n\n**UpstreamRequest** (source/common/router/upstream_request.h/cc):\n\n1. **Connection Pool Phase**:\n   - Request is queued in connection pool if no connection available\n   - Pool creates new connection or reuses idle connection\n   - Once connection ready, `onPoolReady()` is called\n\n2. **Upstream Request Setup**:\n   ```\n   onPoolReady(GenericUpstream upstream, HostDescriptionConstSharedPtr host)\n       ↓\n   Create upstream filter manager (UpstreamFilterManager)\n       ↓\n   acceptHeadersFromRouter() passes request through upstream filters\n       ↓\n   UpstreamCodecFilter sends headers to upstream codec\n       ↓\n   Upstream codec encodes to bytes and sends on connection\n   ```\n\n3. **Upstream Response Phase**:\n   - Upstream codec parses response bytes\n   - Response decoder calls `decodeHeaders()`, `decodeData()`, `decodeTrailers()`\n   - Data passes through upstream filter chain (reverse of downstream)\n   - `UpstreamToDownstream` interface translates to downstream response path\n\n4. **Completion**:\n   - UpstreamRequest tracks per-try timeout and global timeout\n   - On timeout or upstream error: implements retry logic\n   - Retry state decides if request can be retried to different host\n   - After max retries or success, response sent downstream\n\n### Retry Logic\n\n**RetryState** (source/common/router/retry_state_impl.h/cc):\n- Evaluates retry-able errors (connection failure, 5xx status, specific headers)\n- Tracks retry count against configured policy\n- Selects different host on retry to avoid bad endpoints\n- Implements exponential backoff for per-try timeouts\n\n### Timeout Handling\n\n- **Global timeout**: Entire request-response must complete within this time\n- **Per-try timeout**: Each upstream attempt has this timeout\n- **Hedged requests**: If per-try timeout expires, start another request to different host (if configured)\n\n### Shadow Routing\n\nThe router can send \"shadow\" copies of requests to alternate clusters for testing:\n```\nRoute has shadow policy (target cluster + sample rate)\n    ↓\nRouter filter checks if request should be shadowed (random based on sample rate)\n    ↓\nShadowWriter creates secondary upstream request to shadow cluster\n    ↓\nShadow response is discarded (not returned to client)\n    ↓\nOriginal response returned normally\n```\n\n### LoadBalancerContext\n\nThe Filter class implements `Upstream::LoadBalancerContextBase` to provide context for load balancing decisions:\n- Requested cluster info\n- Hash policy and hash key computation\n- Metadata matching criteria\n- Retry state (for host selection during retries)\n- Override host selection\n\n### Source Files\n- **Main Filter**: `source/common/router/router.h` (Filter, FilterConfig classes)\n- **Router Config**: `source/common/router/config_impl.h/cc` (RouteConfiguration parsing)\n- **Route Matching**: `source/common/router/config_impl.h` (RouteEntry, VirtualHost, Cluster match logic)\n- **Upstream Request**: `source/common/router/upstream_request.h/cc`\n- **Retry State**: `source/common/router/retry_state_impl.h/cc`\n- **HTTP Filter Config**: `source/extensions/filters/http/router/config.h/cc`\n\n---\n\n## 4. Cluster Manager and Upstream Connectivity\n\n### Component Responsibility\n\n`ClusterManager` (source/common/upstream/cluster_manager_impl.h/cc) is the subsystem managing upstream clusters and their connection pools. It:\n\n- Maintains cluster definitions and their health state\n- Provides HTTP/TCP connection pools per cluster-host pair\n- Interfaces with load balancers to select healthy hosts\n- Integrates health checking and outlier detection\n- Manages dynamic cluster discovery via CDS (Cluster Discovery Service)\n- Tracks cluster statistics (connection counts, failures, timeouts)\n\n### Cluster Hierarchy\n\n```\nClusterManager\n    ↓\n    Map<cluster_name, ClusterInfo>\n        ↓\n        ClusterInfo:\n            - Cluster configuration (timeout, protocol, TLS settings)\n            - Load balancer instance\n            - Health checker instance\n            - Priority set (primary, secondary, etc.)\n```\n\n### Load Balancing\n\n**Cluster** → **PrioritySet** → **HealthyLoad** → **Host**\n\n1. **Load Balancer Instance** (`Upstream::LoadBalancer`):\n   - Selects host from cluster based on load balancing algorithm\n   - Algorithms: round-robin, least-request, ring-hash, maglev, etc.\n   - Called from router filter with `LoadBalancerContext`\n\n2. **Priority Set**:\n   - Clusters can be organized by priority (primary, backup, etc.)\n   - Load balancer first tries to select from highest-priority healthy hosts\n   - Falls back to lower priorities if higher-priority unavailable\n   - Prevents over-load of primary cluster during failures\n\n3. **Host Selection**:\n   ```\n   LoadBalancer.chooseHost(LoadBalancerContext& context)\n       ↓\n   Compute hash key if using hash policy\n       ↓\n   Apply metadata matching (route metadata + request metadata + connection metadata)\n       ↓\n   Select host from priority set respecting health status\n       ↓\n   Return HostDescriptionConstSharedPtr\n   ```\n\n### Connection Pool Architecture\n\n**HTTP Connection Pool** (`Http::ConnectionPool::Instance`):\n- Per host, per protocol\n- Manages HTTP/1.1, HTTP/2, or HTTP/3 connections to a single upstream host\n- Reuses idle connections\n- Multiplexes multiple streams (for HTTP/2+)\n\n```\nClusterManager::getConnPool(cluster, host, protocol)\n    ↓\nThreadLocalCluster looks up in connection pool map\n    ↓\nIf not found:\n    Create HttpConnPoolImplBase (or HTTP/2 variant)\n    ↓\n    Stores in connection pool map\n    ↓\nHTTP Connection Pool.newStream(ResponseDecoder, Callbacks)\n    ↓\n    If connection available:\n        Attach stream to connection\n        Call Callbacks.onPoolReady()\n    ↓\n    If connection not available but space in queue:\n        Create PendingStream, enqueue\n    ↓\n    If queue full (overload):\n        Call Callbacks.onPoolFailure()\n```\n\n### Connection Lifecycle\n\n**ActiveClient** (managed by HttpConnPoolImplBase):\n```\nCreate connection to host\n    ↓\nCreate codec client (Http1CodecClient or Http2CodecClient)\n    ↓\nEstablish TCP/TLS connection\n    ↓\nFor HTTP/2: send preface and settings\n    ↓\nAccept new streams:\n    For each newStream() request:\n        Get RequestEncoder from codec\n        Attach ResponseDecoder\n        Pass upstream bytes to decoder\n        Return upstream response\n    ↓\nConnection idle timeout → destroy if no active streams\n    ↓\nMax lifetime reached → gracefully drain (complete in-flight, then close)\n```\n\n### Health Checking and Outlier Detection\n\n**Health Checker** (source/common/upstream/health_checker_impl.h/cc):\n- Periodically probes upstream hosts\n- Updates host health status (healthy, degraded, unhealthy)\n- Notifies load balancer when status changes\n\n**Outlier Detection** (source/common/upstream/outlier_detection_impl.h/cc):\n- Monitors request failures to detect failing hosts\n- Ejects unhealthy hosts from load balancer pool\n- Periodically checks if ejected hosts recovered\n- Algorithms: success rate, consecutive failures, HTTP status codes\n\nLoad balancer respects health state:\n```\nLoad Balancer.chooseHost()\n    ↓\n    For each candidate host:\n        If health_status == Healthy: weight = 100%\n        If health_status == Degraded: weight = partial\n        If health_status == Unhealthy: weight = 0% (skip unless no other choice)\n    ↓\n    Select host with probability weighted by health\n```\n\n### Dynamic Cluster Discovery (CDS)\n\nClusters can be added/updated dynamically:\n\n```\nCDS Config Source configured\n    ↓\nClusterManager subscribes to CDS updates\n    ↓\nControl plane sends Cluster proto messages\n    ↓\nClusterManager.addOrUpdateCluster()\n    ↓\n    Parse cluster proto\n    ↓\n    Create new ClusterInfo with appropriate load balancer factory\n    ↓\n    Notify subscribers (e.g., router) of cluster change\n```\n\n### Statistics\n\nConnection pool and upstream statistics tracked:\n- `upstream_cx_total`: Total connections created\n- `upstream_cx_active`: Currently active connections\n- `upstream_rq_total`: Total requests\n- `upstream_rq_pending`: Requests waiting for connection\n- `upstream_rq_time`: Request latency histogram\n- Failures: connect failures, timeouts, reset counts\n- Per-host health status metrics\n\n### Source Files\n- **Main Manager**: `source/common/upstream/cluster_manager_impl.h/cc`\n- **Cluster Info**: `source/common/upstream/upstream_impl.h/cc`\n- **Connection Pools**:\n  - Base: `source/common/http/conn_pool_base.h/cc`\n  - HTTP/1: `source/common/http/http1/conn_pool.h/cc`\n  - HTTP/2: `source/common/http/http2/conn_pool.h/cc`\n- **Load Balancers**: `source/common/upstream/load_*_lb.cc` (various algorithms)\n- **Health Checking**: `source/common/upstream/health_checker_impl.h/cc`\n- **Outlier Detection**: `source/common/upstream/outlier_detection_impl.h/cc`\n\n---\n\n## End-to-End Request Flow\n\n### Complete Request Journey\n\n```\n1. TCP SYN arrives at downstream listener\n   ConnectionManagerImpl.onNewConnection()\n   ↓\n2. Client sends HTTP request bytes\n   ConnectionManagerImpl.onData(data, end_stream)\n   ↓\n3. Codec parses bytes (HTTP/1, HTTP/2, or HTTP/3)\n   Codec.onServerData(Buffer)\n   ↓\n4. Codec emits decoded request\n   ServerConnectionCallbacks.newStream(ResponseEncoder)\n   ↓\n5. ConnectionManagerImpl creates ActiveStream\n   RequestDecoder = ActiveStream\n   ResponseEncoder from codec\n   ↓\n6. Codec calls ActiveStream.decodeHeaders(headers, end_stream)\n   ↓\n7. ActiveStream.decodeHeaders calls FilterManager.decodeHeaders()\n   ↓\n8. FilterManager iterates decoder filters (router is last)\n   Filter A.decodeHeaders() → Filter B.decodeHeaders() → Router.decodeHeaders()\n   ↓\n9. Router filter:\n   - Selects route and cluster\n   - Calls ClusterManager to get connection pool\n   - Creates UpstreamRequest\n   ↓\n10. Connection pool status:\n    If connection available:\n        onPoolReady() called immediately\n    Else:\n        Request queued, waiting for connection\n        On connection ready: onPoolReady() called\n   ↓\n11. UpstreamRequest.onPoolReady():\n    - Creates GenericUpstream (HTTP codec for upstream)\n    - Calls acceptHeadersFromRouter(end_stream)\n    ↓\n12. Data flows through upstream filter chain\n    UpstreamCodecFilter encodes to upstream bytes\n    Bytes sent on upstream connection\n    ↓\n13. Upstream server processes and sends response\n    Response bytes arrive on upstream connection\n    ↓\n14. Upstream codec parses response\n    Calls UpstreamRequest.decodeHeaders() (response)\n    ↓\n15. Router filter translates upstream response to downstream format\n    Calls encodeHeaders() on downstream encoder\n    ↓\n16. FilterManager iterates encoder filters in reverse\n    Filter C.encodeHeaders() → Filter B.encodeHeaders() → Filter A.encodeHeaders()\n    ↓\n17. Last filter's encodeHeaders() calls ResponseEncoder.encodeHeaders()\n    ↓\n18. Downstream codec encodes headers to bytes\n    Sends to client\n    ↓\n19. Upstream response body chunks\n    Each chunk flows through:\n    Router.onUpstreamData(data) → encodeData() → Filter chain → ResponseEncoder\n    ↓\n20. Upstream closes or sends trailers\n    UpstreamRequest.decodeTrailers() called\n    ↓\n21. Router and filter chain process trailers\n    ResponseEncoder.encodeTrailers()\n    ↓\n22. Codec sends trailers to client\n    ↓\n23. Stream complete\n    ActiveStream.completeRequest()\n    Access logs written\n    Metrics updated\n    Stream destroyed\n```\n\n### Request Path Summary\n\n```\nNetwork\n  ↓\nConnectionManagerImpl.onData()\n  ↓\nCodec\n  ↓\nActiveStream.decodeHeaders/Data/Trailers\n  ↓\nFilterManager (decoder filters)\n  ↓\nRouter Filter\n  ↓\nClusterManager + Load Balancer\n  ↓\nHTTP Connection Pool\n  ↓\nUpstream Codec\n  ↓\nUpstream Connection\n```\n\n### Response Path Summary\n\n```\nUpstream Connection\n  ↓\nUpstream Codec\n  ↓\nUpstreamRequest.decodeHeaders/Data/Trailers\n  ↓\nRouter Filter (response translator)\n  ↓\nFilterManager (encoder filters in reverse)\n  ↓\nResponseEncoder\n  ↓\nDownstream Codec\n  ↓\nNetwork (to client)\n```\n\n---\n\n## Extension Points\n\n### 1. Custom Filters\n\nImplement `StreamDecoderFilter`, `StreamEncoderFilter`, or `StreamFilter`:\n\n```cpp\nclass MyCustomFilter : public Http::StreamDecoderFilter {\n  // Process request headers\n  Http::FilterHeadersStatus decodeHeaders(\n      Http::RequestHeaderMap& headers, bool end_stream) override {\n    // Modify headers, check authentication, rate limit, etc.\n    return Http::FilterHeadersStatus::Continue;\n  }\n\n  // Process request body\n  Http::FilterDataStatus decodeData(\n      Buffer::Instance& data, bool end_stream) override {\n    return Http::FilterDataStatus::Continue;\n  }\n};\n```\n\nRegistered via `HttpFilterConfigFactory` and included in HCM config.\n\n### 2. Route Configuration\n\nExtend `RouteConfiguration` to add custom route matching:\n- Custom header matchers\n- Custom metadata matching criteria\n- Custom cluster selection logic\n\n### 3. Cluster Extensions\n\nImplement custom load balancing algorithms via `ThreadAwareLoadBalancer`:\n- Custom selection logic respecting health state\n- Custom host weighting strategies\n\n### 4. Access Loggers\n\nImplement `AccessLog::Instance` to log request/response pairs:\n- Runs after stream completion\n- Access to full request, response, and stream info\n\n### 5. HTTP Codecs\n\nImplement custom codec for new HTTP protocol versions:\n```cpp\nclass MyHttpCodec : public Http::ServerConnection {\n  // Handle new protocol\n};\n```\n\n### 6. Health Checkers\n\nCustom upstream health check logic:\n```cpp\nclass MyHealthChecker : public Upstream::HealthChecker {\n  // Probe upstream hosts\n};\n```\n\n---\n\n## Error Handling\n\n### Codec Errors\nIf codec fails to parse:\n- Exception raised\n- ConnectionManagerImpl catches\n- Local reply: 400 Bad Request or 426 Upgrade Required\n- Connection may be closed\n\n### Filter Errors\nIf filter raises exception during decoding:\n- FilterManager catches\n- Local reply: 500 Internal Server Error\n- Filter is considered in error state\n- Subsequent filters may skip\n\n### Upstream Errors\nIf upstream connection fails:\n- UpstreamRequest.onPoolFailure() called\n- Router evaluates retry policy\n- If retryable: select new host, try again\n- If non-retryable or retries exhausted: send error response (502/503/504)\n\n### Local Reply Flow\nIf a filter (or router) calls `sendLocalReply()`:\n1. Headers and body created\n2. Response encoder calls ResponseEncoder.encodeHeaders()\n3. Downstream codec encodes to bytes\n4. Client receives error response\n5. Stream ends (no further data processing)\n\n---\n\n## Performance Considerations\n\n### Stream Multiplexing\n- HTTP/2+ supports multiple concurrent streams per connection\n- Each stream has independent state, timers, filters\n- Load balancer distributes streams across connection pool\n\n### Connection Pooling\n- Reuse connections to reduce handshake overhead\n- Connection pool limits prevent connection storms\n- Idle timeout prevents resource leaks\n\n### Buffering Strategy\n- Filters can buffer data (e.g., for request body inspection)\n- Watermarks prevent memory exhaustion\n- Small buffers are preferred; large requests chunked\n\n### Timeout Configuration\n- Global timeout: conservative (e.g., 30 seconds)\n- Per-try timeout: shorter (e.g., 5-10 seconds per retry)\n- Allows quick failure detection without excessive latency\n\n---\n\n## Key Interfaces and Their Relationships\n\n```\nNetwork::ReadFilter (ConnectionManagerImpl)\n    ↓ creates\nActive Streams\n    ↓ uses\nFilterManager\n    ↓ chains\nStreamDecoderFilter (router is last)\n    ↓ calls\nRouter Filter\n    ↓ uses\nClusterManager\n    ↓ provides\nLoadBalancer\n    ↓ selects\nHost\n    ↓ provides pool to\nHTTP Connection Pool\n    ↓ creates\nUpstream Codec\n    ↓ sends to/receives from\nUpstream Connection\n```\n\n---\n\n## Related Configuration\n\nKey HCM configuration (envoy/extensions/filters/network/http_connection_manager/v3/http_connection_manager.proto):\n\n- `route_config`: Static route configuration\n- `rds`: Dynamic route discovery config\n- `http_filters`: List of filter configs (order matters for decoder)\n- `access_log`: Access log configuration\n- `common_http_protocol_options`: Timeouts, connection limits\n- `http_protocol_options`: HTTP/1-specific settings\n- `http2_protocol_options`: HTTP/2-specific settings\n- `tracing`: Distributed tracing configuration\n- `stats_matches`: Metrics configuration\n\n---\n\n## Summary\n\nThe HTTP Connection Manager processes requests through a layered architecture:\n\n1. **ConnectionManagerImpl** owns the network connection and creates request streams\n2. **FilterManager** chains request through user-defined filters and the router\n3. **Router Filter** selects the upstream cluster and initiates the upstream request\n4. **ClusterManager** provides connection pooling and load balancing to upstream hosts\n\nEach component has clear responsibilities and well-defined interfaces, enabling Envoy's extensibility through filters, load balancers, health checkers, and codec implementations. The request flows through decoder filters on entry, through the router for cluster selection, through the upstream connection pool, and back through encoder filters on response.\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
